 At that time, TV was not available in every household, so in whose house the TV used to be, whether the old people of the locality, and the children all reached to watch the 'ramayana'
 mejabaan ke ghar main jaise samaaroh jaisaa maahaul ho jaataa tha
 Everyone's feelings were tied in a rosary
 kahin ram kaa rakshason kaa vadh karnaa, hanuman kaa samay par sanjivini laana logon ko romanchit kar jaataa tha, to kahin sitaaharan main sita kaa vilaap yaa sita kaa dharti main samaa janaa unako rulaa detaa tha
 People eagerly await Sunday for the whole week
 'ramayana' ko jis sammaan se hindu dekhte the, usee tarah kaa pyaar or aadar use musalmaan, sikh or anya dharmon se mila
 Its last episode aired on July 31, 1988
 is dedh saal main ram or ramayana bharat ke logon main is tarah bas gaye maano ram bhagwaan na hokar ram lallaa ho gaye, ghar ke ek sadsy jaise
 Realizing the wind's turn, BJP leader LK Advani traveled from Somnath to Ayodhya in 1990 to construct the Ram temple in Ayodhya
 jiskaa aane vaale vakt main bijepi ko bahut phayda hua
 In LK Advani's blog, you can read in the 'yatra' section that it is because of the Somnath Yatra that the BJP has become the largest party in the country today
